    22	}

    40	  const [total, setTotal] = useState(0);

    51

    53	    if (!silent) setLoading(true); else setRefreshing(true);
    54	    let q = supabase.from('profiles')

    56	      .eq('role', 'employee')
    57	      .order(sortKey, { ascending: sortAsc })
    58	      .range(page * PAGE_SIZE, (page + 1) * PAGE_SIZE - 1);
    59	    if (deptFilter !== 'all') q = q.eq('department_id', deptFilter);
    60	    if (statusFilter === 'active') q = q.eq('is_active', true);
    61	    if (statusFilter === 'inactive') q = q.eq('is_active', false);
    62	    const { data, count } = await q;
    63	    setEmployees((data || []) as EmpRow[]);
    64	    setTotal(count || 0);
    65	    if (!silent) setLoading(false); else setRefreshing(false);

    72	      .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'profiles' }, () => fetchEmployees(true))
    73	      .subscribe();
    74	    return () => { supabase.removeChannel(ch); };
    75	  }, [fetchEmployees]);

    87	    });
    88	    setSaving(false);
    89	    if (error || data?.error) { toast.error(data?.error || 'Failed to create employee'); return; }
    90	    toast.success('Employee created successfully');
    91	    newRowId.current = data?.user_id || null;
    92	    setCreateOpen(false);
    93	    form.reset();
    94	    await fetchEmployees(true);
    95	    if (newRowId.current) {
    96	      setHighlightId(newRowId.current);
    97	      setTimeout(() => setHighlightId(null), 2000);
    98	    }
    99	  };
   100	
   101	  const handleEdit = async (v: Partial<EmpRow>) => {
   102	    if (!editEmp) return;
   103	    setSaving(true);

   105	    setSaving(false);
   106	    if (error) { toast.error(error.message); return; }
   107	    toast.success('Employee updated');

   111

   115	    if (error) { toast.error(error.message); return; }
   116	    toast.success('Employee deactivated');

    56	      (counts || []).forEach((c: { department_id: string }) => { countMap[c.department_id] = (countMap[c.department_id] || 0) + 1; });
    57	      rows.forEach(r => { r.member_count = countMap[r.id] || 0; });

   182	                          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="w-7 h-7 text-muted-foreground hover:text-primary" onClick={()=>{setEditAcc(a);editForm.reset({full_name:a.full_name,phone:a.phone||'',department_id:a.department_id||'',designation:a.designation||''});}}><Edit2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5"/></Button>
   183	                          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="w-7 h-7 text-muted-foreground hover:text-destructive" onClick={()=>setDeleteId(a.id)}><Trash2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5"/></Button>
   184	                        </div>
   185	                      </td>
   186	                    </tr>
   187	                  ))}
   188	            </tbody>
   189	          </table>
   190	        </div>
   191	        {totalPages > 1 && (
   192	          <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3 px-4 py-3 border-t border-border">
   193	            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Page {page+1} of {totalPages} · {total} records</p>
   194	            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
   195	              <Button variant="outline" size="icon" className="w-7 h-7" disabled={page===0} onClick={()=>setPage(p=>p-1)}><ChevronLeft className="w-4 h-4"/></Button>
   196	              <Button variant="outline" size="icon" className="w-7 h-7" disabled={page>=totalPages-1} onClick={()=>setPage(p=>p+1)}><ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4"/></Button>
   197	            </div>
   198	          </div>
   199	        )}
   200	      </Card>
   201	
   202	      {/* Create */}
   203	      <Dialog open={createOpen} onOpenChange={setCreateOpen}>
   204	        <DialogContent className="max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] md:max-w-lg">
   205	          <DialogHeader><DialogTitle>Create Management Account</DialogTitle></DialogHeader>
   206	          <Form {...form}><form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(handleCreate)} className="space-y-3 mt-2">
   207	            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-3">
   208	              <FormField control={form.control} name="full_name" rules={{required:'Required'}} render={({field})=>(<FormItem className="col-span-2"><FormLabel className="text-sm font-normal">Full Name</FormLabel><FormControl><Input {...field} placeholder="Jane Smith"/></FormControl><FormMessage/></FormItem>)}/>
   209	              <FormField control={form.control} name="identifier" rules={{required:'Required'}} render={({field})=>(<FormItem><FormLabel className="text-sm font-normal">Email / Username</FormLabel><FormControl><Input {...field} placeholder="jane@company.com"/></FormControl><FormMessage/></FormItem>)}/>
   210	              <FormField control={form.control} name="password" rules={{required:'Required',minLength:{value:6,message:'Min 6 chars'}}} render={({field})=>(<FormItem><FormLabel className="text-sm font-normal">Password</FormLabel><FormControl><Input {...field} type="password" placeholder="••••••"/></FormControl><FormMessage/></FormItem>)}/>
   211	              <FormField control={form.control} name="employee_id" render={({field})=>(<FormItem><FormLabel className="text-sm font-normal">Management ID</FormLabel><FormControl><Input {...field} placeholder="MGT-001"/></FormControl><FormMessage/></FormItem>)}/>
   212	              <FormField control={form.control} name="phone" render={({field})=>(<FormItem><FormLabel className="text-sm font-normal">Phone</FormLabel><FormControl><Input {...field} placeholder="+1 234 567"/></FormControl><FormMessage/></FormItem>)}/>
   213	              <FormField control={form.control} name="department_id" render={({field})=>(<FormItem><FormLabel className="text-sm font-normal">Department</FormLabel><Select onValueChange={field.onChange} value={field.value}><FormControl><SelectTrigger><SelectValue placeholder="Assign dept"/></SelectTrigger></FormControl><SelectContent>{departments.map(d=><SelectItem key={d.id} value={d.id}>{d.name}</SelectItem>)}</SelectContent></Select><FormMessage/></FormItem>)}/>
   214	              <FormField control={form.control} name="designation" render={({field})=>(<FormItem><FormLabel className="text-sm font-normal">Designation</FormLabel><FormControl><Input {...field} placeholder="Department Manager"/></FormControl><FormMessage/></FormItem>)}/>
   215	            </div>
   216	            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 pt-1">
   217	              <Button type="button" variant="outline" className="flex-1 min-w-0" onClick={()=>setCreateOpen(false)}>Cancel</Button>
   218	              <Button type="submit" className="flex-1 min-w-0" disabled={saving}>{saving?'Creating...':'Create Account'}</Button>
   219	            </div>
   220	          </form></Form>
   221	        </DialogContent>
   222	      </Dialog>
   223	
   224	      {/* Edit */}
   225	      <Dialog open={!!editAcc} onOpenChange={v=>!v&&setEditAcc(null)}>
   226	        <DialogContent className="max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] md:max-w-md">
   227	          <DialogHeader><DialogTitle>Edit Management Account</DialogTitle></DialogHeader>
   228	          <Form {...editForm}><form onSubmit={editForm.handleSubmit(handleEdit)} className="space-y-3 mt-2">
   229	            <FormField control={editForm.control} name="full_name" rules={{required:'Required'}} render={({field})=>(<FormItem><FormLabel className="text-sm font-normal">Full Name</FormLabel><FormControl><Input {...field} value={field.value||''}/></FormControl><FormMessage/></FormItem>)}/>
   230	            <FormField control={editForm.control} name="phone" render={({field})=>(<FormItem><FormLabel className="text-sm font-normal">Phone</FormLabel><FormControl><Input {...field} value={field.value||''}/></FormControl><FormMessage/></FormItem>)}/>
   231	            <FormField control={editForm.control} name="department_id" render={({field})=>(<FormItem><FormLabel className="text-sm font-normal">Department</FormLabel><Select onValueChange={field.onChange} value={field.value||''}><FormControl><SelectTrigger><SelectValue placeholder="Select dept"/></SelectTrigger></FormControl><SelectContent>{departments.map(d=><SelectItem key={d.id} value={d.id}>{d.name}</SelectItem>)}</SelectContent></Select><FormMessage/></FormItem>)}/>
   232	            <FormField control={editForm.control} name="designation" render={({field})=>(<FormItem><FormLabel className="text-sm font-normal">Designation</FormLabel><FormControl><Input {...field} value={field.value||''}/></FormControl><FormMessage/></FormItem>)}/>
   233	            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 pt-1">
   234	              <Button type="button" variant="outline" className="flex-1 min-w-0" onClick={()=>setEditAcc(null)}>Cancel</Button>
   235	              <Button type="submit" className="flex-1 min-w-0" disabled={saving}>{saving?'Saving...':'Save Changes'}</Button>
   236	            </div>
   237	          </form></Form>
   238	        </DialogContent>
   239	      </Dialog>
   240	
   241	      {/* View */}

    16	  const [phone, setPhone] = useState(profile?.phone || '');
    17	  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
    18	  const [cropperOpen, setCropperOpen] = useState(false);
    19	  const [uploadingSave, setUploadingSave] = useState(false);
    20	
    21	  const handleSave = async () => {
    22	    setSaving(true);
    23	    const { error } = await supabase.from('profiles').update({ full_name: fullName, phone: phone || null, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() }).eq('id', profile!.id);
    24	    if (error) { toast.error(error.message); } else { toast.success('Profile updated'); await refreshProfile(); }
    25	    setSaving(false);
    26	  };
    27	
    28	  const handleAvatarSave = async (blob: Blob) => {
    29	    setUploadingSave(true);
    30	    try {
    31	      const path = `avatars/${profile!.id}.webp`;
    32	      const { error: uploadErr } = await supabase.storage.from('avatars').upload(path, blob, { upsert: true, contentType: 'image/webp' });
    33	      if (uploadErr) { toast.error(uploadErr.message); return; }
    34	      const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage.from('avatars').getPublicUrl(path);
    35	      // Bust cache with timestamp
    36	      const publicUrl = `${urlData.publicUrl}?t=${Date.now()}`;
    37	      await supabase.from('profiles').update({ avatar_url: publicUrl, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() }).eq('id', profile!.id);
    38	      await refreshProfile();
    39	      toast.success('Profile photo updated');
    40	      setCropperOpen(false);
    41	    } finally {
    42	      setUploadingSave(false);
    43	    }
    44	  };
    45	
    46	  const handleRemoveAvatar = async () => {
    47	    const { error } = await supabase.from('profiles').update({ avatar_url: null, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() }).eq('id', profile!.id);
    48	    if (!error) { await refreshProfile(); toast.success('Profile photo removed'); }
    49	  };
    50	
    51	  return (
    52	    <div className="p-4 md:p-6 space-y-6 min-w-0">
    53	      <div><h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground text-balance">My Profile</h1><p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Personal information and account settings</p></div>
    54	      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
    55	        <Card>
    56	          <CardContent className="p-4 md:p-6 flex flex-col items-center text-center gap-4">
    57	            {/* Avatar with actions */}
    58	            <div className="relative group">
    59	              <Avatar className="w-24 h-24">
    60	                <AvatarImage src={profile?.avatar_url || undefined} />
    61	                <AvatarFallback className="bg-primary/10 text-primary text-xl md:text-2xl">{profile?.full_name?.split(' ').map(n => n[0]).join('').slice(0, 2).toUpperCase()}</AvatarFallback>
    62	              </Avatar>
    63	              <button
    64	                type="button"
    65	                onClick={() => setCropperOpen(true)}
    66	                className="absolute inset-0 rounded-full bg-black/50 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer"
    67	              >
    68	                <Camera className="w-6 h-6 text-white" />
    69	              </button>
    70	            </div>
    71	            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
    72	              <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={() => setCropperOpen(true)} className="gap-1.5 text-xs h-7 px-2.5">
    73	                <Camera className="w-3 h-3" /> Change Photo
    74	              </Button>
    75	              {profile?.avatar_url && (
    76	                <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={handleRemoveAvatar} className="gap-1 text-xs h-7 px-2 text-muted-foreground hover:text-destructive">
    77	                  <Trash2 className="w-3 h-3" />
    78	                </Button>
    79	              )}
    80	            </div>
    81	            <div><h3 className="font-semibold text-foreground">{profile?.full_name}</h3><p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{profile?.employee_id}</p></div>
    82	            <Badge variant="outline" className="border-primary/30 text-primary bg-primary/10 capitalize">{profile?.role}</Badge>
    83	            <div className="w-full space-y-1 text-xs text-left">
    84	              <div className="flex justify-between flex-wrap gap-2 py-1 border-b border-border"><span className="text-muted-foreground">Department</span><span className="text-foreground">{profile?.department?.name || '—'}</span></div>
    85	              <div className="flex justify-between flex-wrap gap-2 py-1 border-b border-border"><span className="text-muted-foreground">Designation</span><span className="text-foreground">{profile?.designation || '—'}</span></div>
    86	              <div className="flex justify-between flex-wrap gap-2 py-1"><span className="text-muted-foreground">Joined</span><span className="text-foreground">{profile?.date_of_joining ? new Date(profile.date_of_joining!).toLocaleDateString() : '—'}</span></div>
    87	            </div>
    88	          </CardContent>
    89	        </Card>
    90	        <Card className="md:col-span-2">
    91	          <CardHeader><CardTitle className="text-sm flex items-center flex-wrap gap-2"><User className="w-4 h-4" />Edit Profile</CardTitle></CardHeader>
    92	          <CardContent className="space-y-4">
    93	            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
    94	              <div><label className="text-sm font-normal text-foreground block mb-1.5">Full Name</label><Input value={fullName} onChange={e => setFullName(e.target.value)} /></div>
    95	              <div><label className="text-sm font-normal text-foreground block mb-1.5">Email</label><Input value={profile?.email || ''} disabled className="opacity-60" /></div>
    96	              <div><label className="text-sm font-normal text-foreground block mb-1.5">Phone</label><Input value={phone} onChange={e => setPhone(e.target.value)} placeholder="+1 234 567 8900" /></div>
    97	              <div><label className="text-sm font-normal text-foreground block mb-1.5">Employee ID</label><Input value={profile?.employee_id || ''} disabled className="opacity-60" /></div>
    98	              <div><label className="text-sm font-normal text-foreground block mb-1.5">Department</label><Input value={profile?.department?.name || '—'} disabled className="opacity-60" /></div>
    99	              <div><label className="text-sm font-normal text-foreground block mb-1.5">Designation</label><Input value={profile?.designation || '—'} disabled className="opacity-60" /></div>
   100	            </div>

   102	          </CardContent>
   103	        </Card>

   108	        onClose={() => setCropperOpen(false)}

     1	import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
     2	import { Clock, Calendar, CheckSquare, Megaphone, DollarSign, LogIn, LogOut } from 'lucide-react';
     3	import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
     4	import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
     5	import { Skeleton } from '@/components/ui/skeleton';
     6	import { toast } from 'sonner';
     7	import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     8	import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
     9	import UpcomingHolidaysWidget from '@/components/common/UpcomingHolidaysWidget';
    10	import { STATUS_LABEL, STATUS_STYLES, deriveAttendanceStatus, timeToMins } from '@/lib/attendanceLogic';
    11	import type { CompanyWorkSchedule, Holiday } from '@/types/types';
    12	
    13	export default function EmployeeDashboard() {
    14	  const { profile, companySettings } = useAuth();
    15	  const [todayAttendance, setTodayAttendance] = useState<{id:string;status:string;check_in_time?:string|null;check_out_time?:string|null;working_hours?:number|null;late_label?:string|null;overtime_hours?:number|null}|null>(null);
    16	  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    17	  const [checkingIn, setCheckingIn] = useState(false);
    18	  const [leaveBalance, setLeaveBalance] = useState<number>(0);
    19	  const [taskCount, setTaskCount] = useState<number>(0);
    20	  const [announcements, setAnnouncements] = useState<{id:string;title:string;content:string;created_at:string}[]>([]);
    21	  const [latestPayroll, setLatestPayroll] = useState<{net_salary:number;month:number;year:number}|null>(null);
    22	  const [liveTime, setLiveTime] = useState('');
    23	  const [schedule, setSchedule] = useState<CompanyWorkSchedule | null>(null);
    24	  const [holidayDates, setHolidayDates] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());
    25	
    26	  const todayDate = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
    27	
    28	  // Load schedule + holidays
    29	  useEffect(() => {
    30	    if (!companySettings) return;
    31	    supabase.from('company_work_schedule').select('*').eq('company_settings_id', companySettings.id).maybeSingle()
    32	      .then(({ data }) => { if (data) setSchedule(data as CompanyWorkSchedule); });
    33	    supabase.from('holidays').select('date').eq('company_settings_id', companySettings.id)
    34	      .then(({ data }) => {
    35	        const s = new Set<string>(); (data as Holiday[]||[]).forEach(h=>s.add(h.date)); setHolidayDates(s);
    36	      });
    37	  }, [companySettings]);
    38	
    39	  useEffect(() => {
    40	    if (!profile) return;
    41	    const fetch = async () => {
    42	      const [attRes, tasksRes, annRes, leaveBRes, payRes, leaveRes] = await Promise.all([
    43	        supabase.from('attendance').select('*').eq('employee_id',profile.id).eq('date',todayDate).maybeSingle(),
    44	        supabase.from('tasks').select('*',{count:'exact',head:true}).eq('assigned_to',profile.id).in('status',['todo','in_progress']),
    45	        supabase.from('announcements').select('id,title,content,created_at').or('is_global.eq.true').order('created_at',{ascending:false}).limit(3),
    46	        supabase.from('leave_balances').select('balance').eq('employee_id',profile.id).limit(4),
    47	        supabase.from('payroll').select('net_salary,month,year').eq('employee_id',profile.id).order('year',{ascending:false}).order('month',{ascending:false}).limit(1).maybeSingle(),
    48	        supabase.from('leave_requests').select('id').eq('employee_id',profile.id).eq('status','approved').lte('start_date',todayDate).gte('end_date',todayDate).maybeSingle(),
    49	      ]);
    50	      // If today is covered by an approved leave and employee hasn't checked in, show on_leave
    51	      const rawAtt = attRes.data;
    52	      const isOnLeaveToday = !!leaveRes.data;
    53	      const todayAtt = rawAtt
    54	        ? (!rawAtt.check_in_time && isOnLeaveToday ? { ...rawAtt, status: 'on_leave' } : rawAtt)
    55	        : (isOnLeaveToday ? { id: 'leave-today', status: 'on_leave', check_in_time: null, check_out_time: null } : null);
    56	      setTodayAttendance(todayAtt);
    57	      setTaskCount(tasksRes.count || 0);
    58	      setAnnouncements(annRes.data || []);
    59	      setLeaveBalance(((leaveBRes.data)||[]).reduce((s:number,b:any)=>s+(b.balance||0),0));
    60	      setLatestPayroll(payRes.data);
    61	      setLoading(false);
    62	    };
    63	    fetch();
    64	  }, [profile, todayDate]);
    65	
    66	  useEffect(() => {
    67	    if (!todayAttendance?.check_in_time || todayAttendance.check_out_time) { setLiveTime(''); return; }
    68	    const interval = setInterval(() => {
    69	      const start = new Date(todayAttendance.check_in_time!).getTime();
    70	      const diff = Date.now() - start;
    71	      const h = Math.floor(diff/3600000), m = Math.floor((diff%3600000)/60000), s = Math.floor((diff%60000)/1000);
    72	      setLiveTime(`${h}:${String(m).padStart(2,'0')}:${String(s).padStart(2,'0')}`);
    73	    }, 1000);
    74	    return () => clearInterval(interval);
    75	  }, [todayAttendance]);
    76	
    77	  const handleCheckIn = async () => {
    78	    setCheckingIn(true);
    79	    const isHoliday = holidayDates.has(todayDate);
    80	    if (isHoliday) { toast.info("Today is a holiday — no need to check in!"); setCheckingIn(false); return; }
    81	    if (todayAttendance?.status === 'on_leave') { toast.info("You have approved leave today — no check-in needed."); setCheckingIn(false); return; }
    82	
    83	    const now = new Date();
    84	    const nowISO = now.toISOString();
    85	
    86	    if (todayAttendance?.check_in_time && !todayAttendance.check_out_time) {
    87	      // Check out with schedule logic
    88	      let updateData: Record<string,unknown> = { check_out_time: nowISO, status: 'present' };
    89	      if (schedule) {
    90	        const d = deriveAttendanceStatus(todayAttendance.check_in_time, nowISO, schedule);
    91	        updateData = { check_out_time: nowISO, status: d.status, working_hours: d.working_hours,
    92	          overtime_hours: d.overtime_hours, early_minutes: d.early_minutes,
    93	          early_label: d.early_label, late_minutes: d.late_minutes, late_label: d.late_label };
    94	      } else {
    95	        const hours = Math.round((Date.now()-new Date(todayAttendance.check_in_time).getTime())/360000)/10;
    96	        updateData = { check_out_time: nowISO, working_hours: hours, status: 'present' };
    97	      }

   100	        toast.success('Checked out successfully');

   102	        setTodayAttendance(data);
   103	      }
   104	    } else if (!todayAttendance) {
   105	      // Check in with schedule logic
   106	      let status = 'present', late_minutes = 0, late_label: string|null = null;

   108	        const startMins = timeToMins(schedule.start_time);
   109	        const nowMins = now.getHours()*60 + now.getMinutes();

   111	          late_minutes = nowMins - startMins;
   112	          if (late_minutes <= schedule.late_threshold_few) late_label = 'Few Minutes Late';
   113	          else if (late_minutes <= schedule.late_threshold_late) late_label = 'Late';
   114	          else late_label = 'Very Late';
   115	          status = 'late';
   116	        }
   117	      } else {
   118	        if (now.getHours() > 9 || (now.getHours()===9 && now.getMinutes()>15)) status = 'late';
   119	      }
   120	      const { data, error } = await supabase.from('attendance')

   122	        .select().maybeSingle();
   123	      if (!error) {
   124	        toast.success(late_label ? `Checked in · ${late_label}` : 'Checked in!');
   125	        setTodayAttendance(data);
   126	      }
   127	    } else {
   128	      toast.info('Already checked out for today');
   129	    }
   130	    setCheckingIn(false);
   131	  };

   134	  const isHolidayToday = holidayDates.has(todayDate);

    95	function getNavItems(role: UserRole): NavItem[] {
    96	  if (role === 'director') return directorNav;
    97	  if (role === 'management') return managementNav;
    98	  // Employees AND interns both use the full employee nav
    99	  return employeeNav;
   100	}
   101	
   102	function getRoleBadgeColor(role: UserRole) {
   103	  if (role === 'director') return 'bg-primary/20 text-primary border-primary/30';
   104	  if (role === 'management') return 'bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/30';
   105	  return 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-400 border-green-500/30';
   106	}
   107	
   108	function getRoleLabel(role: UserRole) {
   109	  if (role === 'director') return 'Director';
   110	  if (role === 'management') return 'Management';
   111	  if (role === 'intern') return 'Intern';
   112	  return 'Employee';
   113	}
